### [37] [Morphological and Star Formation Properties of Cosmic Noon Massive Quiescent Galaxies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02493)
*Vaidik Prasal,Yogesh Wadadekar,Pralay Biswas,Rashi Jain*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 本文利用JWST和HST数据，分析了宇宙正午（2<z<3）时期Abell 2744场中大质量宁静星系的恒星形成与形态特性，发现其呈现内-外熄灭模式、高Sérsic指数（n~4）、紧凑结构（Re≈1.95 kpc），并支持AGN反馈与形态学熄灭共同驱动熄灭过程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解大质量星系在宇宙正午（2<z<3）如何快速转变为宁静状态，及其形态演化与熄灭机制（如AGN反馈、形态学熄灭）之间的关联。

Method: 结合JWST NIRCam宽/中波段与HST归档数据，采用BAGPIPES进行SED拟合筛选宁静星系；用statmorph和pysersic开展形态分析；通过piXedfit进行空间分辨SED建模以获取径向sSFR梯度与形成/熄灭时标剖面。

Result: 识别出14个大质量宁静星系（M*≳10^10 M⊙，sSFR<0.2/t_age）；多数为S0或中间型，中位Sérsic指数n≈4且在z~1.5–4保持稳定；~79%星系显示正向径向sSFR梯度（内低外高），内区比外区早约0.5 Gyr形成、更快熄灭；平均半质量半径Re=1.95±0.13 kpc；部分星系存在微弱AGN活动迹象。

Conclusion: 观测支持‘内-外熄灭’模型，AGN反馈可能主导核心熄灭，而高Sérsic、bulge主导的形态暗示形态学熄灭亦起重要作用；大质量宁静星系的形态早在z~4已建立，并与熄灭状态紧密耦合。

Abstract: We analyze the star formation and morphological properties of massive quiescent galaxies at cosmic noon ($2 < z < 3$) in the Abell 2744 field, using deep JWST NIRCam broad-band and medium-band imaging from the UNCOVER Treasury program and the MegaScience survey, complemented by archival HST data. Using BAGPIPES SED modeling, we select 14 unique massive quiescent galaxies ($M_* \gtrsim 10^{10}$ M$_\odot$, $\mathrm{sSFR} < 0.2/t_\mathrm{age}$). Morphological analysis with statmorph and pysersic reveals that most galaxies are intermediate type or S0s with a median Sérsic index $n \sim 4$, consistent with bulge-dominated systems. This value remains constant over $z \sim 1.5$--$4$, indicating that the morphology of massive galaxies is linked to their quiescence since at least $z \sim 4$. Spatially resolved SED modeling with piXedfit shows that $\sim 79\%$ of galaxies exhibit positive radial sSFR gradients, providing direct evidence for inside-out quenching, with the mean sSFR increasing by $\sim2$ dex from $R/R_e = 0.5$ to $4.5$. Formation time ($t_{50}$) profiles confirm that inner regions formed $\approx 0.5$ Gyr earlier, on average, than the outer regions, and quenching timescale profiles show that the cores were quenched more rapidly than the outskirts. Some galaxies show weak indications of possible AGN activity. Most galaxies are compact, with a mean half-mass radius of $R_e = 1.95 \pm 0.13$ kpc. The observed inside-out quenching pattern and possible AGN signatures are consistent with AGN feedback playing a role in star formation cessation, while the bulge-dominated morphologies suggest morphological quenching may also contribute.

### [38] [Unravelling the complex structure of the Fe II emission region in Type 1 active galactic nuclei](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02508)
*Jelena Kovačević-Dojčinović,Ivan Dojčinović,Luka Č. Popović*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 本文通过分析大量I型活动星系核（AGN）光谱，研究Fe II发射区的复杂结构及其增强机制，发现Fe II等效宽度（EW）与线宽呈反相关，揭示了类星体主序背后的物理本质，并提出Fe II发射区可能存在分层结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解强Fe II发射的原子过程及其在类星体主序中的物理起源。

Method: 利用灵活的Fe II模板将光学Fe II谱线分解为不一致组（Fe II_incons）和一致组（Fe II_cons），后者进一步分为内宽线区（Fe II_ILR）和极宽线区（Fe II_VBLR）成分，并沿类星体主序追踪各成分行为。

Result: 发现Fe II EW与FWHM存在更基本的反相关关系；Fe II_incons和Fe II_ILR的增强主导EW增长，而Fe II_VBLR无明显变化；暗示强Fe II源中Fe II发射区存在分层结构。

Conclusion: 高爱丁顿比可能改变宽线区结构，创造有利于额外原子过程的物理条件，从而激发Fe II_incons线和Fe II_ILR成分，增强光学Fe II辐射。

Abstract: Using a large sample of Type 1 AGN spectra, we investigated the complex structure of the Fe II emission region in order to understand the atomic processes responsible for the enhancement of the Fe II emission. We explored correlations between Fe II features and other spectral parameters, with special focus placed on the quasar main sequence, whose underlying physics is crucial for understanding the origin of the strong Fe II emission. The Fe II emission was modelled using the flexible Fe II template that decomposes the optical Fe II lines into several line groups. According to the atomic properties of transitions, the Fe II lines were divided into inconsistent and consistent groups (Fe II$_{incons}$ and Fe II$_{cons}$), while Fe II$_{cons}$ lines were additionally decomposed into components originating from different parts of the broad-line region (Fe II$_{ILR}$ and Fe II$_{VBLR}$). We traced the behaviour of these line groups and components along the quasar main sequence. Anti-correlation between the equivalent width (EW) of Fe II and the FWHM of Fe II appears to be a more fundamental relation underlying the quasar main sequence. The increase in the EW Fe II for smaller line widths is primarily caused by the strengthening of the EW Fe II$_{incons}$ lines and, with a smaller contribution, by the enhancement of the EW Fe II$_{ILR}$ components, while the EW of Fe II$_{VBLR}$, on average, does not significantly change along the quasar main sequence. The results indicate a possible stratification of the Fe II emission region occurring in sources with strong Fe II emission. An increased Eddington ratio may modify the broad-line region structure, leading to specific physical conditions suitable for triggering additional atomic processes. This may result in the appearance of Fe II$_{incons}$ lines and FeII$_{ILR}$ components, which consequently increase the optical Fe II strength.

</details>


### [39] [Using Ly$α$ Transmitted Spectrum to Probe IGM Transmission and Identify Ionized Structures in Cosmic Reionization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02539)
*Weida Hu,Casey Papovich,Lu Shen,Pablo Arrabal Haro,Bren E. Backhaus,Nikko J. Cleri,Mark Dickinson,James S. Dunlop,Steven L. Finkelstein,Mauro Giavalisco,Anton M. Koekemoer,Vasily Kokorev,Sara Mascia,Lorenzo Napolitano,Laura Pentericci,Aaron Smith,Anthony J. Taylor,Xin Wang,L. Y. Aaron Yung*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 本研究利用JWST/NIRSpec对143个高红移星系（5<z<7）进行光谱观测，直接测量了4.5<z<6.5宇宙时期星系视线方向上的星系际介质（IGM）透射率，并在GOODS-S场中发现一个z~5.75–6的高电离‘气泡’结构，其IGM透射率显著高于平均值，且与已知的大尺度星系过密区相关。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索再电离时期星系际介质（IGM）的电离状态和空间结构，特别是利用高信噪比星系光谱作为探针，弥补传统类星体探针在空间覆盖和统计样本上的不足。

Method: 基于JWST/NIRSpec棱镜光谱数据，对CAPERS和JADES巡天中143个z=5–7星系开展Lyα蓝翼通量分析，结合SED建模估计固有紫外连续谱，从而直接计算各星系视线方向的IGM透射率；重点分析GS-18846（z=6.335）的高信噪比光谱以识别异常高透射结构，并结合其环境星系分布进行空间关联分析。

Result: 1）星系平均IGM透射率与类星体结果一致；2）在GOODS-S场发现一个z~5.75–6、尺度达~110 cMpc（线视向）及≥21×17 cMpc²（横向）的高透射‘气泡’，其透射率T=0.17±0.02，比同红shift平均值高一个数量级；3）该气泡与已知星系过密区共处，其成员星系表现出增强的Lyα可见性与更宽的等效宽度分布。

Conclusion: 高信噪比星系光谱是探测再电离时期电离结构（如HII气泡）的有效新工具；Lyα过密可能示踪高IGM透射区域，但需进一步区分环境效应对星系本身性质的影响。

Abstract: We present a study of intergalactic medium (IGM) transmission at $4.5 < z < 6.5$ using high-signal-to-noise JWST/NIRSpec prism spectroscopy of 143 galaxies at $5<z<7$ from the CAPERS and JADES surveys. By comparing the observed flux blueward of Ly$α$ emission line to the prediction of spectral energy distribution modeling, we directly measure the IGM transmission along the individual galaxy sightlines. The average transmission measured from these galaxy sightlines is consistent with previous measurements based on luminous quasars. Current NIRSpec spectroscopy is sufficiently deep to probe IGM transmission on single sightlines. We find evidence for a highly ionized structure, \bubble, at $z\sim 5.75-6$ in the GOODS-S field based on the analysis of a high-S/N spectrum of one galaxy, GS-18846, at $z=6.335$. The IGM transmission of GS-z6IS is $0.17\pm0.02$, an order of magnitude higher than the average of previous measurements at this redshift. This structure has a line-of-sight scale of $\sim110$ cMpc and spatially extends over at least $21\times17$ cMpc$^2$. GS-z6IS is associated with a known large-scale galaxy overdensity at the same redshift, whose member galaxies show enhanced Ly$α$ visibility and a broader Ly$α$ equivalent width distribution compared to field galaxies at similar redshift. This result supports the interpretation that Ly$α$ overdensity can trace bubbles of increased IGM transmission, although environmental effects on galaxy properties may also contribute. Our study demonstrates that high-S/N galaxy spectra offer a powerful new approach to tracing ionized structures during the epoch of reionization.

### [40] [A Virgo Environmental Survey Tracing Ionised Gas Emission (VESTIGE). XXI. Statistical properties of individual HII regions in perturbed galaxies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02648)
*A. Boselli,M. Fossati,Y. Roehlly,M. Boquien,J. Braine,P. Cote,J. C. Cuillandre,B. Epinat,L. Ferrarese,S. Gwyn,G. Hensler*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 本研究利用VESTIGE巡天的窄带Hα+[NII]成像数据，分析了385个室女座星系团中电离气体发射星系的HII区性质，重点比较了HI气体亏损（受环境扰动）与气体富足（未受扰动）星系的差异，发现扰动星系的HII区光度函数更陡、特征光度更高，且HII区数量密度在星系外盘显著降低，支持‘热气体压强剥离HI并由外向内抑制恒星形成’的星系演化机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究星系团环境中HI气体亏损（受扰动）星系与场星系在HII区统计和物理性质上的差异，以理解环境驱动的星系演化机制，特别是ram pressure stripping对恒星形成的抑制作用。

Method: 基于VESTIGE巡天的窄带Hα+[NII]成像数据，识别322个恒星形成星系中的76645个HII区；构建复合光度函数、直径分布、电子密度分布及多种标度关系；按HI-deficiency参数分组，重点对比扰动（HI亏损）与未扰动（气体富足）星系，并聚焦于有效半径以外的外盘区域。

Result: HI亏损星系的HII区光度函数具有更陡的暗端斜率和更高的特征Hα光度；其单位恒星质量和单位盘面面积的HII区数量更低，且该差异随HI-deficiency增大而增强，主要体现在外盘；外盘HII区显著缺失。

Conclusion: 观测结果支持ram pressure stripping主导的星系演化模型：ICM相互作用由外向内剥离HI气体，导致外盘恒星形成率先被抑制，从而改变HII区的整体分布与统计性质。

Abstract: We use narrow-band Halpha+[NII] imaging data gathered during VESTIGE, a blind survey of the Virgo cluster carried out with MegaCam at the CFHT, to identify HII regions in 385 galaxies showing ionised gas emission. We identify 76645 HII regions in 322 star-forming galaxies and study their physical properties for those above the completeness limit (L(Ha)>=10^37 erg s-1). The present work is focused on perturbed cluster galaxies, identified as those having a reduced amount of HI when compared to similar objects in the field. We derive composite luminosity functions, diameter and electron density distributions, and several scaling relations, and compare them to those already derived for gas-rich, unperturbed systems identified during the VESTIGE survey. The analysis shows that the statistical and physical properties of HI gas-deficient cluster galaxies are different from those of unperturbed systems, with perturbed objects having a steeper faint-end slope and a brighter characteristic Ha luminosity than gas-rich galaxies. The difference in the two distributions comes principally from the outer disc (outside the effective radius). The analysis of the scaling relations indicates that perturbed objects have a lower number of HII regions per unit stellar mass and disc surface than unperturbed systems, with differences increasing with the HI-deficiency parameter, principally in the outer disc where HII regions are less present in gas-poor systems. All these differences can be explained in the framework of galaxy evolution in rich environments, where their hydrodynamic interaction with the surrounding ICM (ram pressure) removes the gas outside-in quenching the star formation activity in the outer disc once the HI is removed.

### [41] [Jet-driven shocks and turbulence in radio-loud Active Galactic Nuclei observed with JWST MIRI/MRS](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02663)
*Rogemar A. Riffel,Gabriel L. Souza-Oliveira,Luis Colina,Almudena Alonso-Herrero,Marina Bianchin,Kalliopi M. Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 本文利用JWST观测七个近邻射电噪AGN，研究射电喷流与星际介质（ISM）的相互作用，发现喷流不仅沿喷流轴、还在垂直方向上驱动分子和电离气体的湍流，并以激波主导H₂转动谱线激发，表明喷流是调控多相ISM运动学与激发的关键机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解AGN小尺度喷流-ISM相互作用对核区物理与运动学的影响，区别于大尺度射电模反馈。

Method: 基于JWST/MIRI/MRS对七个近邻射电噪AGN的观测，结合空间分辨的H₂/PAH通量比与电离气体谱线比（如[FeII]、[NeII]、[NeIII]），约束H₂激发机制并评估喷流对多相气体的影响。

Result: 喷流在分子与电离气体中均引发增强湍流，且作用范围超出准直喷流通道；H₂/PAH比、H₂激发温度与激波敏感电离气体示踪体强相关，表明激波主导H₂转动谱线激发。

Conclusion: 射电喷流是近邻射电噪星系中多相ISM运动学与激发的关键驱动因素。

Abstract: Jet-cloud interactions are a key manifestation of Active Galactic Nucleus (AGN) feedback on nuclear scales, distinct from the large-scale radio-mode feedback that suppresses gas cooling in galaxy halos. On these smaller scales, radio jets can inject energy and momentum into the interstellar medium (ISM), shaping the physical and kinematic properties of the nuclear and circumnuclear regions of galaxies. Using JWST MIRI/MRS observations of seven nearby radio-loud AGN (3C293, 3C305, Centaurus A, Cygnus A, IC5063, NGC1052, and M87), we investigate jet-driven turbulence in both the warm molecular and ionized gas phases. By combining spatially resolved H$_2$/PAH flux ratios with diagnostic line ratios of the ionized gas, we constrain the dominant H$_2$ excitation processes and assess the impact of radio jet--ISM interactions on the multiphase gas. We find that radio jets drive enhanced turbulence in both molecular and ionized (traced by [FeII], [NeII] and [NeIII] lines) gas, not only along but also perpendicular to the jet axis, indicating that jet--ISM interactions extend beyond the collimated jet channel and affect the nuclear environment. Strong correlations between the H$_2$/PAH ratio, the H$_2$ excitation temperature, and shock-sensitive ionized-gas tracers indicate that jet-driven shocks dominate the excitation of the H$_2$ rotational lines in most sources. These results indicate that radio jets are a key driver of multiphase ISM kinematics and excitation in nearby radio-loud galaxies.

### [42] [AGN STORM 2. XII. Ground-Based Optical Photometry and Lag Measurements of Mrk 817](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02875)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决活动星系核中普遍存在的‘吸积盘尺寸差异’问题，即观测到的光学/紫外连续谱反响延迟远大于标准薄盘再处理模型预测值，并探究其物理起源（如BLR贡献、遮蔽效应等）。

Method: 基于AGN STORM 2项目，利用地面望远镜在uBgVriz波段开展高时间采样（g波段中位间隔0.4天）成像监测；以Swift卫星UVW2波段（1928 Å）为参考，采用ICCF、JAVELIN和PyROA三种方法测量各波段连续谱反响延迟；将整个观测期分为三个光度与遮蔽性质不同的子时期进行对比分析。

Result: ICCF测得的延迟在u到z波段为3.0±0.8至7.9±1.5天，符合τ ∝ λ^{4/3}关系；JAVELIN和PyROA结果系统偏短且偏离该幂律；所有延迟比薄盘再处理模型预测大3–6倍；三个子时期间延迟变化达因子2，最大延迟出现在最亮、最蓝、X射线遮蔽最弱的第一阶段。

Conclusion: Markarian 817的连续谱延迟不仅受吸积盘再处理主导，还显著受到宽线区弥散连续谱辐射或中心引擎与宽线区之间遮蔽外流变化的影响；电离光度短期变化可导致延迟大幅改变，挑战纯几何/热模型解释。

Abstract: We present the ground-based imaging campaign and light curves of Markarian 817 as part of the multiwavelength monitoring program AGN STORM\,2. Observations were carried out over 1.4 years in \emph{uBgVriz} filters, with a median cadence of 0.4 days in \emph{g}. Reverberation lags are measured using three methods (ICCF, JAVELIN, and PyROA) with the Swift UVW2 band (1928 Å) as the reference light curve. The ICCF centroid lags range from $3.0\pm0.8$ days for the $u$ band up to $7.9\pm1.5$ days for $z$, and are consistent with a $τ\propto λ^{4/3}$ dependence, the relation expected for lamp-post reprocessing by a Shakura-Sunyaev disk. Lags measured with the other methods are systematically shorter, and deviate from a $λ^{4/3}$ power-law spectrum at long wavelengths. The lags exceed thin-disk reprocessing predictions by factors of $\sim$3-6, similar to the ``disk size discrepancy'' seen in other Seyfert galaxies. We divide the campaign into three epochs with different levels of mean luminosity and X-ray obscuring column density and find that the lags vary by as much as a factor of 2 between epochs. The intrinsic spectral energy distribution is bluer and brighter during the first third of the campaign, and the longest continuum reverberation lags are obtained during that period. These results suggest that changes in ionizing luminosity can produce large variations in continuum lags on short timescales by altering the diffuse continuum luminosity emitted by the broad-line region and/or obscuring outflow, although changes in obscuration between the central engine and broad-line region may also contribute to the lag variations.

</details>

### [43] [Recommendations for the Astronomy Graduate Admissions Process](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00992)
*Emily M. Levesque,Courtney D. Dressing,Rachel Ivie,Grace Krahm,Meredith A. MacGregor,Daniel R. Piacitelli,Tom Rice*

Main category: astro-ph.IM

TL;DR: 本文提出了改进和标准化天文学研究生招生流程的建议，包括统一申请材料格式（如推荐信、申请论文、简历和非正式成绩单）以及明确招生时间表（如鼓励4月1日为申请人‘筛选截止日’）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有天文学研究生招生流程虽大体相似，但小范围要求差异及沟通与透明度不足，给学生和项目都带来挑战。

Method: 基于美国天文学会（AAS）研究生招生特别工作组（GATF）报告，由AAS研究生招生工作组（WGGA）提出简明、可行的招生流程改进建议。

Result: 提出了统一的申请材料组成（两封500词推荐信、一篇1500词申请论文、CV、非正式成绩单）和更清晰透明的招生时间安排（如推广4月1日为‘down-select date’）。

Conclusion: 通过标准化申请内容与加强沟通透明度，可显著降低学生与招生项目的负担，提升天文学研究生招生公平性与效率。

Abstract: As the AAS Working Group on Graduate Admissions (WGGA) we are sharing brief recommendations for improving and standardizing key elements of the graduate admissions process in astronomy. Most astronomy graduate programs have large areas of overlap in their admissions processes; however, the existing small variations in requirements and mismatches in communication and transparency make admissions more challenging for students and programs alike. To improve this situation, and building on the work presented in the AAS Graduate Admissions Task Force (GATF) report we recommend a few simple and straightforward changes for application content, communication, and timelines. These include an application format that consists of 1) two 500-word recommendation letters, 2) one 1500-word application essay, 3) an applicant CV, and 4) unofficial transcripts; and an admissions timeline that includes effective and transparent communication from programs and encouraging an April 1st "down-select date" for applicants.

</details>


### [44] [The Outer Space Treaty Won't Save Us From Ourselves](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01019)
*John Barentine,Aparna Venkatesan*

Main category: astro-ph.IM

TL;DR: 本文探讨了外层空间活动激增引发的伦理与哲学问题，尤其是空间军事化问题，指出《外空条约》（OST）虽具理想性但缺乏有效执行机制，已难以应对当前公私利益带来的压力；作者主张将太空法律上认定为‘环境’，以此为基础构建以和平合作共治为导向的新治理路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 外空活动迅速增长引发空间军事化等伦理危机，《外空条约》因执行力弱、依赖缔约方善意而面临失效风险，亟需新的法律与伦理框架。

Method: 通过分析现行国际空间法（特别是《外空条约》）的局限性，结合 terrestrial 伦理理论（威慑伦理 vs. 协议伦理），提出将太空法律定义为‘环境’的规范性主张，并援引地球环境治理中的合作实践作为类比范例。

Result: 论证了将太空视为法律意义上的‘环境’可为强化其保护提供更坚实基础，并识别出若干基于和平合作共治原则的潜在治理路径。

Conclusion: 唯有确立太空作为受法律保护的‘环境’地位，才能兼顾伦理正当性与人类理性自保需求，从而在关键历史节点上维护太空的长期完整性与和平利用。

Abstract: The rapid growth of human activities in outer space sounds urgent alarms around ethical and philosophical issues, particularly concerning space militarization. The present international legal framework governing activities in space, the Outer Space Treaty (OST), views the peaceful exploration of space for scientific research as co-equal to other 'uses' entitled to "due regard" with respect to "potentially harmful interference" on the part of other space actors. The OST is deeply aspirational but has weak enforcement mechanisms, relying at its core on the goodwill of all involved parties as the fundamental basis for accountability. But that framework now faces unsustainable pressures from both public and private interests, and current agreements like the OST may be unable to exert timely, material protections. Terrestrial frameworks of "ethics of deterrence" versus the "ethics of agreements" are quickly expanding into cosmic environments. We argue for the legal recognition of space as an environment as the basis of any future approach to securing its integrity, and share examples of agreements grounded in peaceful cooperative stewardship of shared environments. These represent potential pathways forward that are ethical and also serve rational self-interest and self-preservation at this crucial juncture for humanity.

</details>


### [45] [Status of the COSmological Microwave Observations CALibrator](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01057)
*L. Mousset*

Main category: astro-ph.IM

TL;DR: COSMOCal项目旨在通过在地球静止轨道部署人工偏振源，为CMB望远镜提供高精度校准参考，目前已完成初步仪器开发及2026年地面校准测试。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着CMB望远镜灵敏度提升，亟需更高精度的校准手段；现有校准源难以满足亚度级偏振角精度需求。

Method: 设计并研制可在地球静止轨道运行的人工偏振校准源，工作频点为90、150和270 GHz，偏振方向精度优于0.1度，并开展地面校准实验验证。

Result: 已完成2026年3月在法国空间天体物理研究所（IAS）的校准实验，验证了关键性能指标；项目自2022年起推进，目前处于仪器研制阶段。

Conclusion: COSMOCal为下一代CMB实验提供了可行的、高精度的在轨偏振校准方案，有望显著提升CMB偏振测量的系统误差控制能力。

Abstract: As the sensitivity of CMB telescopes increases, the need for precise calibration becomes critical. Started in 2022, the COSMOCal project aims to place an artificial polarized source in geostationary orbit, which will serve as a reference for CMB telescopes. This source will emit at 90, 150 and 270 GHz and will be linearly polarized with a highly precise orientation smaller than 0.1 deg. This proceeding presents the scientific motivations for the project, the current status of the development of the instrument and the results of a calibration campaign performed in March 2026 at the Institut d'Astrophysique Spatiale.

</details>


### [46] [Statistically Significant Linear Alignments Among High-Confidence Transient Candidates on POSS-I Photographic Plates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01190)
*Brian Doherty*

Main category: astro-ph.IM

TL;DR: 本文在POSS-I巡天数据中发现了7组高置信度瞬变源的线性排列和空间异常聚集，这些现象无法用已知天体或人工卫星解释，且与核试验时间地点存在潜在关联。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索POSS-I历史影像中未被识别的异常瞬变现象，检验是否存在非自然或未知物理机制导致的特殊空间分布模式。

Method: 使用机器学习分类器筛选107,875个候选体，选取概率≥0.50的36,215个进行线性对齐（≤3角秒宽度）和近距离成对（<30角秒）统计检验，并通过蒙特卡洛模拟评估显著性；结合轨道动力学、地理投影及背景分布（如黄道面）排除常见天体污染。

Result: 发现7块底片上存在5–8个源的显著线性排列（p < 0.03），其中6组在地球表面投影后保持恒定经度（p ~ 3e-10）；4组集中于美国中部（−96°），1组紧邻汉福德核试验场且日期吻合；近距离成对率是随机预期的16.2倍，且与线性事件同夜发生（p < 0.0001）；高置信瞬变明显避开黄道面，排除小行星等常见源。

Conclusion: 这些瞬变现象极可能源于一类未知的、高海拔、缓慢移动的非自然光源，其特性与冷战早期高空核试验活动存在时空关联，挑战现有天体物理学与航天史认知。

Abstract: I report the detection of statistically significant linear alignments and anomalous spatial clustering among high-confidence transient candidates in the VASCO catalog of vanishing sources on Palomar Observatory Sky Survey (POSS-I) photographic plates (1949-1957). A machine learning classifier scores 107,875 candidates by their likelihood of being genuine transients. Searching the 36,215 candidates with probability >= 0.50 for collinear groupings narrower than 3 arcsec, I find 7 plates with alignments of 5-8 sources that exceed Monte Carlo expectations (p < 0.03, 10,000 iterations). The aligned sources are point-like, not streaks, which rules out any continuously luminous object crossing the field during the 45-minute exposures. The implied angular rates (1-15 arcsec/s) overlap with the geosynchronous regime but are inconsistent with low or medium Earth orbits, and no artificial satellites existed during the POSS-I era. When I project each alignment onto Earth's surface assuming a high-altitude object, 6 of 7 maintain constant geographic longitude with sub-degree spread (combined p ~ 3e-10). Four of these cluster near -96 deg longitude (central United States); one falls within 0.3 deg of the longitude of the Hanford nuclear production site on a nuclear test window date. Close pairs (< 30 arcsec) occur at 16.2x the random rate, and the nights with alignments are the same nights with excess close pairs (Fisher exact p < 0.0001). Plate artifacts cluster near the ecliptic plane (26%), but high-confidence transients are depleted there (16%; chi-square test p = 3.3e-82), which rules out asteroids, comets, and zodiacal debris as the dominant source. No transient reappears at the same sky position on a different night. All of these transients predate Sputnik 1.

</details>


### [47] [Design, Testing, and Commissioning of the Sun Yat-sen University (SYSU) 80 cm Infrared Telescope](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02339)
*Zhong-Nan Dong,Bin Ma,Chun Chen,Wei-Sen Huang,Jin-Ji Li,Jia-Qi Lin,Yun Shi,Hao-Ran Zhang,Duo-Le Cao,Bao-Gang Chen,Tai-Ran Deng,Rui-Chen Gao,Yi Hu,Hong-Zhuang Li,Xia Li,Pu Lin,Yang Liu,Bo Ma,Rong-Feng Shen,Li-Duo Song,Fang-Yu Xu,Hao-Nan Yang,Yan Yu,Jun Yuan,Xiang-Tao Zeng,Hao-Yuan Zheng*

Main category: astro-ph.IM

TL;DR: SYSU 80 cm望远镜是位于中国冷湖（海拔4100米）的新型近红外时域天文观测设备，采用反射式Cassegrain设计，配备J/K波段Nasmyth焦点；其J波段成像系统初期使用商用InGaAs相机（Mars640），后升级为科学级深冷YNAOIR相机，实现背景极限探测，单次20秒曝光达J~17 mag（Vega），30分钟叠加达J~19.4 mag，亮源（J~14 mag）测光精度达毫星等量级；已成功观测GRB、超新星、彗星、AGN、z>6类星体及褐矮星等，并实现J~20.5 mag深场成像，验证了InGaAs相机在天文观测中的可行性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 发展适用于高海拔、面向时域天文的国产近红外专用望远镜，并验证新兴InGaAs红外相机在专业天文观测中的实用性与性能潜力。

Method: 建设并调试一台80 cm口径、Cassegrain光学结构、双Nasmyth焦点的近红外望远镜；分阶段部署并对比测试商用InGaAs相机（INS Mars640）与科学级深冷InGaAs相机（YNAOIR）的暗电流、读出噪声、极限星等与测光精度；开展多类天体实测（暂现源、变源、深场）以评估系统性能。

Result: YNAOIR相机实现暗电流~14 e-/s/pix、读出噪声~11 e-，单次20 s曝光达J~17 mag（Vega），30分钟叠加达J~19.4 mag；对J~14 mag目标实现毫星等测光精度；成功观测GRB、SNe、彗星、AGN、z>6类星体、褐矮星及J~20.5 mag深场。

Conclusion: SYSU 80 cm望远镜及其InGaAs成像系统已成功运行，证实InGaAs技术可支撑高质量近红外时域与深度巡天观测，为国内乃至国际发展低成本、高性能近红外天文设施提供了可行路径与重要范例。

Abstract: The Sun Yat-sen University (SYSU) 80 cm telescope is a new generation near-infrared (NIR) facility in China dedicated to time-domain astronomy, while also serving as a testbed for emerging NIR cameras. Commissioned in October 2024 at the 4100 m Lenghu site on the Tibetan Plateau in China, the telescope adopts a reflective Cassegrain design with two Nasmyth foci for J and K bands. The J band imaging system, initially equipped with a 640 x 512 off-the-shelf InGaAs camera (INS Mars640) and upgraded in June 2025 to a 1280 x 1024 science-grade, deeply cooled camera (YNAOIR), achieves background-limited performance with a dark current of ~ 14 e-/s/pix and a readout noise of ~ 11 e-. The system reaches a limiting magnitude of J ~ 17 mag (Vega system) in single 20 s exposures and depths of J ~ 19.4 mag with stacked 30 minute exposures. For a variable with J ~ 14 mag during on-sky tests, the system delivers millimagnitude-level photometric precision. Since commissioning, the telescope observed transients such as gamma-ray bursts (GRBs), supernovae and comets, variables including active galactic nuclei (AGNs), high-redshift quasars (z > 6), and brown dwarfs, as well as deep-field imaging reaching J ~ 20.5 mag. This validates the feasibility of using InGaAs cameras for astronomical observations, encouraging other institutions to develop dedicated infrared telescopes or integrate infrared cameras into existing optical telescopes.

</details>


### [48] [Operating the Fabry-Pérot systems of the European Solar Telescope in multi-aperture mode](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02687)
*G. B. Scharmer,M. G. Löfdahl,J. de la Cruz Rodríguez,B. Lindberg,H. Socas-Navarro,D. Kiselman,M. Rempel,J. Leenaarts*

Main category: astro-ph.IM

TL;DR: 本文提出在欧洲太阳望远镜（EST）尚未启用多共轭自适应光学系统（MCAO）的初期运行阶段，采用多孔径模式（将4.2米主镜光学分割为六个1.4米子孔径）以提升图像质量，尤其利于高时间分辨率的偏振光谱观测；该方案仅需低成本改造现有法布里-珀罗成像系统镜头，具备快速切换、波长自适应和系统无侵入等优势，并通过仿真与图像重建验证其可行性与效益。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: EST在首年运行时缺乏高空视宁度补偿的MCAO系统，导致其空间分辨能力可能不如更小口径望远镜；亟需一种低成本、低风险的临时方案来提升科学产出，特别是对稳定高质量时序偏振光谱数据的需求。

Method: 提出并设计EST多孔径运行模式：将4.2 m主镜光学分割为6个1.4 m子孔径；仅修改三套法布里-珀罗成像系统（覆盖380–860 nm）的相机镜头；开展数值模拟与模拟数据的图像重建实验；提供简化的光学设计方案。

Result: 多孔径模式可显著降低高空视宁度引起的波前误差RMS，使后处理图像复原更可靠；实现持续稳定的高图像质量，满足高时间分辨率偏振光谱观测需求；支持各FPI系统独立、快速地在全孔径与多孔径模式间切换，且对主/次光学系统及FPI本体无影响。

Conclusion: 多孔径方案是一种可行、灵活、低成本的过渡策略，能在MCAO部署前大幅提升EST的科学数据质量与数量；仿真与重建结果证实其有效性，为EST早期科学运行提供了重要支撑。

Abstract: We discuss how to optimise the science output of the European Solar Telescope (EST), when used without the wide-field compensation for high-altitude seeing that the EST multi conjugate adaptive optics (MCAO) will offer. This will be the mode of operating EST during its first year(s). Without MCAO, the spatial resolution of a much smaller telescope could surpass that of EST. We therefore propose to operate EST in multi-aperture mode, by optically segmenting the 4.2 m aperture into six 1.4 m subapertures, until MCAO is operational. Operating at smaller aperture diameter pushes down the root mean square wavefront errors from the high altitude seeing to levels that can more reliably be compensated for in restored images using post processing methods. This will significantly improve image quality. In particular, the multi-aperture mode will provide the sustained stable high image quality needed for obtaining time sequences of spectropolarimetric data. The multi-aperture mode is implemented with low-cost modifications of the camera lenses of the three Fabry-Perot systems that will be used to cover the wavelength range 380--860~nm. Switching between the full-aperture and multi-aperture modes can be done quickly and independently for the three FPI systems. This allows flexible optimisation of EST, taking into account that the seeing is much better at long wavelengths than at short wavelengths, without any impact on the EST primary or secondary optical systems or on the actual FPI systems. The multi-aperture addition to EST provides a powerful and flexible option that has the potential of significantly improving the quality and amount of its science data before MCAO is operational. In this publication, we perform simulations and image reconstructions of simulated data to demonstrate the benefits of the multi-aperture option, and provide a simple optical design to demonstrate its feasibility.

</details>


### [49] [PDRS : A Linear $\mathcal{O}(N)$ Algorithm for Segmentation of High-Activity Regions in Irregularly Sampled Time Series](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02843)
*Atal Agrawal*

Main category: astro-ph.IM

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种线性时间复杂度O(N)的算法Peak-Driven Region Segmentation (PDRS)，用于在不规则采样的天文时序数据中快速识别高活动性暂现区域，相比传统O(N²)的Bayesian Blocks方法显著提升效率，并在多类实际数据上验证了其有效性与通用性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于Bayesian Blocks的方法计算复杂度为O(N²)，难以应对ZTF和LSST等大规模巡天项目产生的海量、不规则采样光变曲线；亟需高效、可扩展的替代方案。

Method: PDRS算法以统计显著的局部极大值为种子，通过梯度感知的多源广度优先搜索进行区域扩张，并结合鞍点合并与中值滤波抑制虚假检测。

Result: 在SDSS Stripe 82和ZTF DR23的类星体与活动星系核光变曲线测试中，PDRS能以远低于Bayesian Blocks的计算成本，识别出与其相当的高活动性候选区域。

Conclusion: PDRS是一种高效、鲁棒、领域无关的时序分段算法，不仅适用于天文暂现源探测，还可推广至生物医学信号、地震记录和工业传感监控等领域。

Abstract: Identifying transient high-activity episodes in astronomical time series requires partitioning data into regions of distinct statistical behavior. A widely adopted approach combines Bayesian Blocks with a hill-climbing procedure to isolate high-activity regions, but carries $\mathcal{O}(N^2)$ complexity -- a scalability challenge for wide-field surveys like ZTF and the upcoming Rubin Observatory (LSST), where light curves routinely contain thousands of irregularly sampled observations. We present Peak-Driven Region Segmentation (PDRS), a linear-time $\mathcal{O}(N)$ algorithm for rapid extraction of high-activity regions in irregularly sampled data. PDRS seeds candidate regions at statistically significant local maxima and expands them via a gradient-aware multi-source breadth-first search. Saddle-point merging and a median-based filter suppress spurious detections. Functioning as a computationally efficient pre-processing stage, PDRS isolates candidate transient events for downstream analysis. We demonstrate its efficacy on quasar light curves from SDSS Stripe~82 and AGN light curves from ZTF DR23, showing that PDRS identifies candidate high-activity regions comparable to those from Bayesian Blocks at substantially reduced cost. Its domain-agnostic formulation and physically interpretable parameters make PDRS broadly applicable beyond astronomy, including biomedical signals, seismic recordings, and industrial sensor monitoring.

</details>


### [50] [Role of General Users in the Lifecycle of Scientific Software](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02870)
*Bjorn Emonts,the CASA Team*

Main category: astro-ph.IM

TL;DR: 本文探讨了在资源有限的情况下，如何通过用户参与来优化科学软件（如CASA）的生命周期管理，强调用户需求与开发优先级的协调。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 科学软件开发常受限于资源，内部项目目标与终端用户（普通用户）需求不一致，导致软件难以广泛普及。

Method: 基于射电天文领域Common Astronomy Software Applications（CASA）的软件生命周期实践，分析用户参与开发优先级制定及支持的可行路径。

Result: 提出在资源受限条件下，软件团队可通过结构化方式吸纳用户和用户群体参与需求反馈与功能优先级排序，从而提升用户满意度与开发效率。

Conclusion: 用户深度参与软件生命周期（尤其在需求定义与开发排序阶段）可实现双赢：既满足用户实际期望，又增强软件可持续性与社区影响力。

Abstract: In science, the lifecycle of software products is typically managed with limited resources while facing unlimited demand. Scientific software requirements are necessarily often dominated by internal project specifications and deadlines, but these internal priorities, while beneficial for the community as a whole, do not always align with the individual needs of our ultimate customers: general users. For software products to have the broadest reach, ideally the general user community should be involved in all aspects of the data lifecycle, but reality is that user expectations need to be managed. Based on the lifecycle of the Common Astronomy Software Applications for radio astronomy (CASA), we will show avenues for software teams to interact with general users, even when facing limited resources for user support. We will discuss how involvement of users and user groups in prioritizing software development can benefit both the user community and the software teams. The contents of these proceedings were presented at the 35th conference on Astronomical Data Analysis Software & Systems (ADASS XXXV).

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: We study the use of transformers to reconstruct the compositions of tensor products of two-dimensional rational conformal field theories (RCFTs) based on their low-energy spectra. We further demonstrate that our method generalizes to CFTs with larger central charge and unseen classes of RCFTs by adding a small number of out-of-domain examples. Our results show that transformers are effective at this task and point towards a new tool for bulk reconstruction in AdS/CFT.

### [56] [Finite-temperature operator basis on $\mathbb{R}^3 \times S^1$ for SMEFT](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02878)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用虚时间形式，在ℝ³×S¹时空流形上应用Hilbert级数方法；严格施加分部积分与运动方程约束（仅沿空间方向）；并分析电/磁场旋度为零、时间分量规范选取等额外约束的影响；最后将算符映射到静态三维空间及零温SMEFT算符表示。

Conclusion: 本文提供了有限温度下SMEFT的首个系统性、可扩展的算符分类框架，为热早期宇宙、重离子碰撞等高温物理场景中的有效理论分析奠定了基础。

Abstract: We present the first complete non-redundant operator basis for the Standard Model Effective Field Theory (SMEFT) at finite temperature, using the imaginary-time formalism. By employing the Hilbert series method on the space-time manifold $\mathbb{R}^3 \times S^1$, we classify all effective operators up to dimension-six. In constructing the basis, we consistently impose integration-by-parts and equations-of-motion constraints along spatial directions. We further analyze the impact of additional constraints, including the vanishing of the curl of the electric and magnetic fields and gauge choices for the temporal components on an operator basis. We also express them in terms of static three-dimensional spatial and zero-temperature SMEFT operators. At dimension five and six, we identify intrinsically thermal operators that vanish in zero temperature. Our framework is fully general and extends to arbitrary mass dimension and compact connected internal symmetry groups.

### [57] [Hidden gauge invariance](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01453)
*Karl-Henning Rehren*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文通过自主方法重新审视规范不变性的作用，不预先假设规范不变性，而是从量子原理（特别是希尔伯特空间上的表示）出发推导出标准模型粒子的可重整相互作用；结果发现大多数满足约束的相互作用具有‘隐藏’的精确且未破缺的规范不变性，并可在无需不定态空间和鬼场的情况下统一处理有质量与无质量矢量玻色子。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 重新审视规范不变性在标准模型中的基础作用，避免人为预设规范对称性，寻求更基本的量子原理（如希尔伯特空间表示）来约束相互作用形式。

Method: 采用自主相互作用方法，以量子力学基本原理（尤其是作用于希尔伯特空间的表示）为唯一约束，推导可重整相互作用；引入弦局域化相互作用以保障S矩阵的弦无关性，并与传统规范理论的S矩阵等价。

Result: 发现绝大多数满足量子约束的相互作用天然具备一种可通过量子场重定义揭示的‘隐藏’规范不变性；该不变性严格成立且未破缺，即使存在有质量矢量玻色子；由此可在正定希尔伯特空间中构建一致的粒子物理理论，无需不定度规或鬼场。

Conclusion: 规范不变性并非基本假设，而是量子原理和希尔伯特空间结构所蕴含的派生性质；标准模型相互作用可基于更基础的量子原则重建，摆脱对规范冗余和不定态空间的依赖。

Abstract: The role of gauge invariance is reconsidered by "deriving it without assuming it" within an autonomous approach to interactions of Standard Model particles. In this approach, the renormalizable interactions are purely constrained by quantum principles, notably the representation on a Hilbert space. It is shown that - surprisingly - most interactions fulfilling the constraints enjoy a "hidden" gauge invariance (uncovered via redefinitions of quantum fields). The hidden gauge invariance is exact and unbroken even in the presence of massive vector bosons. While the Hilbert space formulation requires the use of "string-localized interactions", its role is to secure that S-matrices are string-independent, and in fact coincide with S-matrices with local interactions from the gauge theory approach on indefinite state spaces. Thus, particle physics with massless and massive vector bosons can be understood without neither indefinite state spaces nor ghosts.

</details>


### [58] [Reductions in Khovanov-Rozansky operator formalism](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01584)
*D. Galakhov,E. Lanina,A. Morozov*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种新的Khovanov-Rozansky (KhR) 不变量的双复形描述方法，用局部构造的算子D和共轭映射χ^(±)替代了传统的矩阵分解，使计算更直观、局部化，并支持多种简化策略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统Khovanov-Rozansky理论中矩阵分解概念反直觉且不易操作，亟需一种具有清晰物理意义、更局部化、可简化计算的新表述。

Method: 引入局部定义的幂零算子D（作用于MOY分解图的每个顶点）及简单共轭映射χ^(±)连接不同分解；将KhR构造拆解为两步：先取D的‘垂直’上同调（置于超立方体顶点），再由χ^(±)定义边上的态射并计算‘水平’上同调；利用局部性实现图的简化（如Reidemeister变换、反平行锁结构）。

Result: 建立了具有局部算子与态射的KhR双复形框架；实现了对N=2及任意N的二部图情形下从双复形到类Khovanov单复形的全局约化；揭示了反平行锁结构对二部图计算简化的关键作用。

Conclusion: 该工作将KhR理论重述为物理意义更清晰、构造更局部、计算更灵活的双复形语言，不仅统一理解原有结构，还拓展了可约化情形，为 knot invariant 的计算与推广提供了新工具。

Abstract: Sophisticated Khovanov-Rozansky (KhR) description of knot invariants in the fundamental representation can be reformulated in terms of bicomplex with a simple physical meaning. Namely, the counterintuitive matrix factorization is substituted by simple operators $D$, locally constructed for every MOY resolution of a link diagram, which becomes nilpotent when the diagram has no external lines. Operators for different resolutions are related by equally simple conjugations $χ^{(\pm)}$. The KhR procedure then splits in two steps - defining ``vertical'' cohomologies of $D$, which are associated with particular resolutions and will be put at vertices of the hypercube, and conjugations $χ^{(\pm)}$, that define morphisms along its edges. As usual, standard combinations of morphisms are nilpotent, and one can define ``horizontal'' cohomologies - which are then combined into Poincaré polynomial, called KhR polynomial in application to links. This construction remains global in the sense that resulting cohomologies depend on the entire link diagram, but all its building blocks, including the operators and morphisms are local in the sense that they are defined for its particular vertices. Sometimes, this allows simple local reductions, allowing to eliminate or change particular vertices or sets of those. Along with the obvious case of Reidemeister equivalencies this happens also for antiparallel-lock tangles, what is responsible for simplification of bipartite calculus. In the $N=2$ and arbitrary $N$ bipartite cases, one can also provide global reductions transferring the local construction of the KhR double-complex to the global construction of the Khovanov(-like) single-complex.

</details>

Abstract: We define a higher-derivative generalization of Maxwell-Chern-Simons theory in $\mathcal{N}=1$ and $\mathcal{N}=2$ superspaces. *Ichiro Oda*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文在二次引力的协变正则形式框架下，探讨了破坏S矩阵幺正性的质量幽灵粒子的禁闭问题，提出通过BRST四重态机制使质量幽灵与Faddeev-Popov幽灵形成束缚态，从而将其禁闭于零范数态中以恢复幺正性；并指出该质量幽灵的渐近场表现为质量偶极子，而其束缚态则满足质量Klein-Gordon方程，类比于QCD中的色禁闭。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决二次引力理论中因质量幽灵导致的S矩阵幺正性破缺问题。

Method: 基于Bonora和Tonin的超场公式，在协变正则形式框架下，利用BRST四重态机制分析质量幽灵与Faddeev-Popov幽灵的束缚态及其渐近行为。

Result: 证明若存在质量幽灵与Faddeev-Popov幽灵的束缚态，则质量幽灵可通过BRST四重态机制被禁闭于零范数态中，从而恢复幺正性；且其渐近场为质量偶极子，束缚态满足质量Klein-Gordon方程。

Conclusion: 质量幽灵可通过与Faddeev-Popov幽灵形成束缚态实现禁闭，类比QCD中（可能）被禁闭的质量胶子，为二次引力的幺正性提供新机制。

Abstract: In the framework of the covariant canonical formalism of quadratic gravity, we consider the problem of confinement of massive ghost which violates the unitarity of the physical S-matrix. It is shown that if there is a bound state between the massive ghost and Faddeev-Popov ghost the massive ghost is confined in the zero-norm states through the BRST quartet mechanism, thereby the unitarity being restored. Based on the superfield formulation by Bonora and Tonin, we show that the asymptotic field of the massive ghost must be a massive dipole whereas that of the bound state obeys a massive Klein-Gordon equation. This situation may be of some similarity to color confinement in quantum chromodynamics (QCD) where it is conjectured that not a massless but a massive gluon is in fact confined.

</details>


### [62] [All DDF/lightcone two-particle decay widths up to level $8$ in open bosonic string in critical dimension](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02013)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: We carry out an ``experimental analysis'' in which we explicitly compute all possible Abelian two-particle decay channels (excluding the tachyon) of open bosonic massive states up to level (8), amounting to approximately 2,000,000 cases. The aim is to develop intuition about which states are the most stable and to identify the dominant decay channels. Our results show that, for all levels considered, the ratio of decay widths between the slowest- and fastest-decaying states is of order one. In most cases, the dominant polarized decay channel accounts for at least $10\%$ of the total decay width, while the first five channels together contribute roughly 60%. Even when we sum about $10000$ polarized channels. Dominant polarized channels always involve at least one photon and all strings ultimately decay into a photon carrying energy at the string scale. The most stable states are made using the DDF/lightcone oscillators $A_{-1}$ and some $A_{-2}$ and are close relatives of the states on the leading Regge trajectory. Finally, we discuss how the computation on the lightcone differs from the equal-time computation due to ``surges'', i.e., decays into a tachyon and a higher-mass state, and we hypothesize that, in bosonic string theory, decays into tachyons constitute the dominant decay channels.

Abstract: We complete the analysis of planar Makeenko--Migdal loop equations in the continuum limit. Using the confining twistor-string representation, we compute the quantum fluctuation determinant. In Minkowski space, this reduces to a discrete product of finite-dimensional matrix quadratures. The $ζ$-regularized weight is independent of winding number $w$. Near the mass shell, the pole singularity is generated by $w \to \infty$, suppressing fluctuation variance as $1/w$. The holonomy shift $h$ dictates exact geometric degeneracies between parity families, reproducing mass splittings without phenomenological spin-orbit parameters. Evaluated one-loop residues yield relative transition cross-sections, demonstrating nontrivial topology- and flavor-dependent scaling that captures heavy-mass quenching and phase-space enhancement for high-spin light states.For the pure Yang--Mills closed string, we demonstrate dynamical stability of the pure-gauge minimal surface in the planar limit: the conformal Liouville anomaly drives the string strictly to the trigonometric minimum ($q=0$). The complex elliptic geometry analytically collapses, yielding linear Regge trajectories. The translation zero-mode measure dynamically nullifies the transition amplitude of the massless scalar ghost, providing an explicit analytic mechanism for a purely gluonic mass gap. Abstract: We analyze a simple extension of the Schwinger model, which we refer to as the $p$-Schwinger model, on a de Sitter background. In Minkowski space, the $p$-Schwinger model has discrete zero- and one-form global symmetries that are spontaneously broken, yielding $p$ degenerate ground states. We demonstrate that these features persist upon placing the $p$-Schwinger model on a global de Sitter background, establishing that such discrete global symmetries can be spontaneously broken for quantum field theories in de Sitter space. In particular, the theory is endowed with $p$ distinct, but locally-indistinguishable, de Sitter invariant states, the de Sitter vacua, satisfying the Hadamard property. We couple a variant of the $p$-Schwinger model with ${\rm N}_{\rm f}$ flavors to quantum gravity with $Λ>0$, and demonstrate the existence of a semiclassical de Sitter saddle at large ${\rm N}_{\rm f}$. In the gravitational theory, the $p$ de Sitter invariant vacua are speculatively interpreted as microstates of the de Sitter horizon in the low-energy effective field theory.

</details>

*Edward A. Mazenc,Debmalya Sarkar*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文探讨了扭曲全息理论中的开-闭-开三重性，通过在解析的conifold上研究两组横向D膜，得到了两个等价的开弦描述，并展示了其如何精确捕捉D膜对几何的反作用，从而直接诊断涌现的体时空。

Result: 证实开弦有效势精确刻画另一组膜对几何的反作用；将探针膜作用量与变形conifold中的巨引力子匹配；第二开弦描述可直接诊断涌现的体时空。

Abstract: We explore the ideas of open-closed-open triality within twisted holography. Starting from two transverse stacks of branes in the B-model on the resolved conifold, we obtain two equivalent open string descriptions. Both are full-fledged field theories. In the appropriate limit, they simplify to gauged $βγ$-systems with determinant insertions, as expected from open string field theory. The $ρ$-matrix models that have appeared previously in the literature appear from an on-shell analysis of the field-theory actions. Most importantly, we show that the effective potential generated by integrating out the open strings on the other stack of branes exactly captures their backreaction on the geometry. In particular, we match the action of the probe branes to that of giant gravitons in the $\textit{deformed}$ conifold. The second open string description of the triality thus directly diagnoses the emergent bulk spacetime.

We also explore SPCs for events with tip-tip and body-body collision configurations, which further support these findings.

### [74] [Three-flavor supernova neutrino simulation using a hybrid quantum-classical algorithm with qutrits](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01099)
*Daniel J. Heimsoth,A. Baha Balantekin,Pooja Siwach*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种混合经典-量子算法，在三能级量子计算机（qutrit）上模拟超新星核心坍缩中的自相互作用三味中微子系统；该方法基于Dirac-Frenkel变分原理，利用qutrit Hadamard测试估算哈密顿量中幺正算符的期望值，进而构造时间演化算符，后续演化则在经典计算机上完成；结果表明该混合算法在t≈30ω₀⁻¹内与精确数值积分高度一致，并优于量子Trotter分解法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统纯经典数值模拟在处理大规模、强非线性中微子集体振荡时面临计算复杂度高、难以刻画量子相干性的挑战；而全量子模拟受限于当前硬件规模和噪声；因此需探索兼具可行性与物理保真度的混合量子-经典方案。

Result: 在时间步长δt = 0.005 ω₀⁻¹下，混合算法成功模拟至t ≈ 30 ω₀⁻¹，结果与精确数值解高度吻合；验证了该方法在中微子集体振荡动力学中的有效性与稳定性；并指出其相比量子Trotter化具有更优的资源开销与误差控制特性。

Conclusion: 混合经典-量子算法是当前中微子量子多体模拟的一种可行且具优势的路径；它规避了全量子线路深度过大与噪声敏感问题，同时比纯经典方法更能自然嵌入量子相干机制；为未来中微子味转化模拟提供了新的计算范式。

Abstract: We simulate a self-interacting three-flavor neutrino system within a core-collapse supernova using a hybrid classical-quantum algorithm on a qutrit computer. Based on the Dirac-Frenkel evolution equations, we employ a variation of the quantum-assisted simulator (QAS) to calculate the system's time evolution operator by performing qutrit Hadamard tests to find expectation values of unitary operators in the Hamiltonian. The time evolution simulation is then done classically. We find that the hybrid algorithm produces results comparable to an exact numerical integration out to times of $t \approx 30 \,ω_0^{-1}$ with time step $δt = 0.005 \,ω_0^{-1}$, where $ω_0$ is the energy scale of the single neutrino vacuum oscillations. We discuss the lessons learned in simulating neutrino systems using this hybrid quantum-classical algorithm, along with the advantages it offers over quantum Trotterization.

Abstract: $X(2370)$ falls in the mass region of the lowest pseudoscalar glueball predicted by lattice QCD studies and its decay properties are similar to those of $η_c$. A previous lattice QCD study finds that the pseudoscalar glueball ($G_{0^-}$) and the lowest pseudoscalar charmonium ($c\bar{c}(0^-)$) can mix with a small mixing angle $\sinθ$. It is therefore possible that $X(2370)$ and $η_c$ are admixtures of $G_{0^-}$ and $c\bar{c}(0^-)$. In this picture, although $\mathrm{Br}(J/ψ\toγη_c)$ is insensitive to the small $\sinθ$, $\mathrm{Br}(J/ψ\to γX(2370))$ can be enlarged drastically by the mixing due to the much larger kinematic factor for $J/ψ\to γX(2370)$ and the much larger transition form factor for $J/ψ\to γ(c\bar{c}(0^{-}))$. Depending on the value of $\sinθ$, $\mathrm{Br}(J/ψ\to γX(2370))$ can be much larger than that of the pure pseudoscalar glueball, namely, $2.3(8)\times 10^{-4}$ that is predicted by a quenched lattice QCD calculation. Present results by BESIII favor a small mixing angle of $\mathcal{O}(1^\circ)$, which can be further constrained by more measurements of $X(2370)$ decays if the mixing picture applies here.

Once the singlet scalar is coupled to standard model fermions, CP-violating phases become observable through EDMs. We analyze whether current and future EDM experiments can probe the parameter region where the GW signal is detectable by SKA and THEIA. We find that the current electron EDM bound already constrains part of the parameter space, while future sensitivities at the level of $10^{-31}$--$10^{-32}\,e\,\mathrm{cm}$ can probe regions overlapping with the GW-detectable domain. We investigate whether the $Δ$SM can account for these triboson excesses through electroweak production and decay of triplet scalars. We find that while current data prefers a non-zero new physics signal ($2.6σ$), the $Δ$SM predicts more events than observed, such that it is consistent with data but not preferred over the SM. ### [79] [Probing Saturation Effect in Heavy Meson Pair Correlation in Forward $pA$ Collisions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01527)

Main category: hep-ph

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 在Color Glass Condensate有效理论框架下，对重介子对关联引入统一的Sudakov重求和，以压制大对数发散并提高微扰计算可靠性，结合核PDF与小x演化，计算前向pA中D̄D、B̄B等关联及核修正因子RpA。

In this work, we study heavy meson pair correlation in forward proton-nucleus collisions by incorporating a unified Sudakov resummation for heavy meson pair correlations in the Color Glass Condensate effect theory. Our results are in good agreement with the $Δφ$ data measured by the LHCb Collaboration for $D^0 \bar D^0$ pairs in forward $pp$ and $pA$ collisions, as well as $J/ψ$ pairs from $b\bar b$ decays in forward $pp$ collisions. Furthermore, we present predictions for $D\bar D$ and $B\bar B$ correlations in the forward rapidity regions at the Large Hadron Collider. A pronounced mass-hierarchy is observed in the nuclear modification factor, $R_{pA}\big|_{m_b}<R_{pA}\big|_{m_c}$, indicating stronger sensitivity to saturation effects at small $x$. As the rapidity increases, the suppression becomes more pronounced while the mass hierarchy remains robust. This study will help us to search for the saturation signal via heavy-meson pair correlations in forward $pA$ collisions.

### [80] [Multimodal Fragmentation of All-Heavy Pentaquarks: Uncertainty-Aware Predictions for Hadron Colliders](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01539)

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为准确预言全粲五夸克态在高能对撞机上的产生截面，需同时刻画微扰QCD演化与非微扰结构模型带来的不确定度，尤其针对其多模态碎裂行为。

Method: 构建多模态共线碎裂函数PQ5Q1.1；采用缺失高阶变分（F-MHOUs）估计微扰不确定度，通过调控横向动量波函数结构（F-NPWF）建模非微扰不确定度，并在类复制框架中统一处理；改进初始尺度下组分粲夸克碎裂输入以涵盖紧致多夸克与二夸克机制；结合(sym)JETHAD接口进行NLL/NLO⁺精度计算。

Result: 给出了HL-LHC与FCC能量下五夸克+喷注联合产生的不确定性可控预言；明确了底夸克类似研究需更精细非微扰建模，留待后续工作。

Conclusion: 该框架成功连接了奇特强子结构、重味碎裂物理与高能QCD，为未来实验探测全粲五夸克态提供了首个具备完整不确定度评估的理论工具。

Abstract: We present an uncertainty-aware description of leading-power fragmentation for all-charm pentaquark states ($S$-wave $|cccc\bar{c}\rangle$) at hadron colliders. We construct a multimodal set of collinear fragmentation functions, PQ5Q1.1, incorporating both perturbative and nonperturbative uncertainties. Perturbative effects are estimated via missing higher-order variations (F-MHOUs), while the nonperturbative wave function is modeled through controlled modifications of its transverse-momentum structure (F-NPWF), consistently combined within a replica-like framework. The initial-scale input for constituent charm fragmentation is refined to describe both compact multiquark and diquark-driven production mechanisms. We employ the (sym)JETHAD interface to study NLL/NLO$^+$ semi-inclusive pentaquark-plus-jet production at the HL-LHC and future FCC. The bottom sector is left to future dedicated studies due to its enhanced sensitivity to nonperturbative modeling. Our results provide a flexible framework for uncertainty-controlled predictions, bridging exotic-hadron structure, heavy-flavor fragmentation, and high-energy QCD.

### [81] [Equation of State of Dense Matter: Pauli Degeneracy, Pairing Correlations, and Implications for Neutron Stars](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01618)

Method: 基于温度远小于费米能的条件，自然分离出Sommerfeld、费米液体和配对区域，构建统一的状态方程（EOS），并代入Tolman-Oppenheimer-Volkoff方程求解中子星结构。

Conclusion: 该统一EOS可改善中子星质量-半径关系的理论预测，并有助于解释现代天文观测结果。

Abstract: We develop a unified description of dense fermionic matter that consistently incorporates Pauli degeneracy, interaction effects, and pairing correlations. The condition that the temperature is much smaller than the Fermi energy leads to a natural separation between Sommerfeld, Fermi-liquid, and pairing regimes, and how these contributions enter the equation of state. The resulting EOS is applied to the Tolman-Oppenheimer-Volkoff equations to analyze neutron-star structure. We demonstrate that Pauli degeneracy provides the dominant pressure, interactions determine the stiffness of the EOS, and pairing correlations produce subleading but potentially significant corrections, especially in quark matter. Implications for mass--radius constraints and modern observations are discussed.

Abstract: Equations of a boost-invariant and cylindrically symmetric perfect hydrodynamics are solved numerically for initial conditions inspired by the wounded nucleon model. The energy-momentum and spin tensors are used in the form that describes a relativistic massive gas governed by Boltzmann statistics. In contrast to one dimensional boost-invariant expansion, we find a coupling between the azimuthal and longitudinal components of the electric and magnetic components of the spin polarization tensor. This feature is similar to that found earlier for the Gubser symmetry, however, our treatment allows for a more general form of initial conditions and expansion geometry. Defining the freeze-out hypersurface by the constant temperature condition, we evaluate the Pauli-Lubański four-vector and find that for the assumed geometry the only nonzero total polarization may be induced by the longitudinal component of the magnetic part of the spin polarization tensor coupled with the azimuthal electric component. The obtained results may serve as a reference point for more realistic models of hydrodynamic expansion.

In the same region, stau is realized to be another light supersymmetric particle, and some of the solutions can be inconsistently lighter. We find that it can weigh as light as about 600 GeV consistently, and it can be tested also soon over its lifetime. We summarize and also exemplify our findings with five benchmark scenarios. Most of the benchmark solutions also reveal that the solutions can be tested in heavy Higgs boson searches, which shape the whole Higgs boson spectrum in models.

### [88] [Pair creation via Amplitude-Modulated Periodic and Quasiperiodic Pulse Sequences](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02515)
*Deepak Sah*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了交替符号电场脉冲序列驱动的非微扰对产生现象，比较了周期性与斐波那契准周期性脉冲序列对动量谱和粒子产额的影响，发现时间长程有序可作为调控多脉冲施温格对产生的有效参数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索时间结构（尤其是长程有序）如何调控强场量子电动力学中的非微扰粒子对产生过程，为高强激光实验中设计优化脉冲序列提供理论依据。

Method: 采用量子动理学方法，分析具有严格周期性（E₁,E₂循环）和斐波那契准周期性（由斐波那契替代规则生成）电场脉冲序列下的纵向动量谱与粒子产额。

Result: 周期序列产生类多缝干涉谱；斐波那契序列导致谱碎片化与部分动量空间局域化；N=20时效应更显著；粒子产额对场强比呈强非线性依赖，准周期序列在强场下略高于周期序列；总产额主要由等效场强决定，而谱形由时间有序主导。

Conclusion: 时间长程有序是调控多脉冲施温格对产生的有效控制参量，该结论为未来高强激光实验中脉冲序列设计提供了理论指导。

Abstract: We study nonperturbative pair production driven by alternating-sign electric field pulse trains. Using a quantum kinetic approach, we analyze both the longitudinal momentum spectrum and the particle yield for pulse sequences with either strictly periodic temporal structure, in which the pulse amplitudes alternate in a regular and repeating (E_1, E_2) pattern, or quasiperiodic (Fibonacci-ordered) structure, where the amplitudes follow a deterministic but aperiodic sequence generated by the Fibonacci substitution rule, exhibiting long-range order without exact repetition. For N=12 pulses, periodic trains generate regularly modulated spectra characteristic of multi-slit (Ramsey-type) interference, whereas Fibonacci sequences produce fragmented structures and partial momentum-space localization. Increasing the pulse number to N=20 further enhances these effects: periodic driving yields sharper and higher-contrast interference fringes, while quasiperiodic ordering leads to stronger localization and increasingly irregular spectral features.The particle yield exhibits a strongly nonlinear dependence on the field-strength ratio. For weak modulation , both temporal orderings produce nearly identical yields. For stronger fields, a modest crossover behavior is observed, with quasiperiodic sequences yielding slightly larger values than the periodic case. Overall, temporal ordering primarily redistributes spectral weight in momentum space, while the integrated yield is governed predominantly by the effective field strength. These results establish long-range temporal ordering as an effective control parameter in multipulse Schwinger pair production and provide guidance for designing tailored pulse sequences in future high-intensity laser experiments.

</details>


### [89] [Detectability of Magnetar-Induced Vacuum Birefringence with IXPE and eXTP](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02541)
*Fayez Abu-Ajamieh*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用磁星真实磁场剖面模型，结合Adler积分公式计算偏振本征模（平行与垂直分量）的时间延迟和相位差，并计算所有已知磁星的Stokes参数。

Result: 时间延迟比文献中先前估计大一个数量级；IXPE和eXTP均能定量测量磁星真空双折射；1RXS J170849.0-400910是最具潜力的探测候选体。

Abstract: We analyze the prospects of quantitatively detecting vacuum birefringence from magnetars using the IXPE and eXTP experiments. We adopt a realistic profile to model the magnetic field of magnetars, and use it to calculate the time delay and phase difference in the parallel and perpendicular components of polarization eigenmodes using Adler's integral formula. We find that the time delay could be an order of magnitude larger than previous estimates in the literature. We also calculate the Stokes parameters for all known magnetars and show that both IXPE and eXTP are capable of quantitatively measuring birefringence from magnetars, with the magnetar dubbed 1RXS J170849.0-400910 being the best candidate for detection.

*Pasquale Di Bari*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决宇宙学观测与中微子振荡实验之间存在的中微子质量张力，以及解释宇宙射电背景过剩等未解之谜。

Method: 分析中微子不可见衰变、辐射衰变及引入‘回旋镖机制’（即可见扇区与暗扇区在不同时期交换粒子）来调和观测矛盾，并评估其对中微子有效磁矩和21 cm信号的影响。

Result: 提出回旋镖机制可规避中微子磁矩实验上限约束，预测的有效磁矩有望被下一代实验探测，并预期对21 cm宇宙学信号有可观测贡献。

Conclusion: 中微子物理，尤其是涉及暗扇区的新机制，为探索超越标准模型（BSM）的宇宙学现象提供了激动人心的新途径。

Abstract: In this talk I discuss how neutrinos might help solving or alleviating different anomalies and tensions in cosmology. Invisible decays of the heaviest relic neutrinos might provide a way to solve the neutrino mass tension between cosmological observations and neutrino oscillation experiments. The excess radio background mystery could be explained by radiative decays of relic neutrinos. However, the upper bound on the neutrino effective magnetic moment requires some trick to be circumvented. To this extent, I discuss a recently proposed boomerang mechanism in which the visible sector throws dark neutrinos into the dark sector at $t \sim 100\,{\rm s}$ and $T \sim 100\,{\rm keV}$, and much later (basically at the present time) the dark sector throws back photons into the visible sector. The mechanism predicts an effective neutrino magnetic moment that might be within the reach of next experiments. Some contribution to the 21 cm cosmological signal is also expected. These are exciting times for cosmological searches of BSM physics.

</details>


### [91] [Studying the Infrared Behaviour of Improved Logarithmic Accuracy Parton Showers with Herwig](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02622)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 提升偶极子喷注算法的精度，并研究其在不同能区（特别是红外区）对强子化模型的影响，以改善事件生成器的整体物理表现。

Method: 在Herwig事件生成器中实现并比较两种新提出的具有次领头对数精度的偶极子喷注算法，与现有偶极子和角序喷注算法进行对比；开展NLO匹配和簇强子化研究；分析红外截断定义对强子级可观测量的影响；进行参数拟合与可调性分析。

Result: 发现新算法不仅在对数区域性能更优，在硬区（NLO匹配）和红外区（强子化初始条件）也起关键作用；不同红外截断导致强子级结果显著差异；确定了各模型的最佳拟合参数。

Conclusion: 红外截断的精确定义是连接部分子喷注与强子化模型的关键环节，应作为后续研究喷注-强子化协同效应的出发点；新偶极子喷注算法具备更好理论精度与实际可调性。

Abstract: We have implemented two recently proposed dipole shower algorithms that have next-to-leading-logarithmic accuracy at leading colour in the Herwig event generator. We study their properties and compare them to Herwig's existing dipole and angular ordered parton shower algorithms. In addition to their improved properties in the logarithmic regime, we find important roles for their extrapolations into the hard regime, where we perform NLO matching, and into the infrared regime, where we perform cluster hadronization. We emphasise the importance of this infrared regime and the precise definition of the infrared cutoff used by each shower as the initial state for Herwig's hadronization model. Studying the results at the hadron level, we find important consequences of this infrared cutoff difference and propose it as a starting point for further study of the interplay between parton showers and hadronization models. We conclude by studying the models' tunability and identifying the best-fit parameters for each.

### [93] [Collins asymmetries for pion-in-jet production in polarized $\ell p$ collisions at the EIC](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02890)
*Umberto D'Alesio,Carlo Flore,Marco Zaccheddu*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了极化轻子-质子碰撞中喷注内π介子产生的Collins方位角不对称性，采用简化TMD方法，利用从DIS和e+e−湮灭中提取的横动量依赖的横自旋分布和Collins碎裂函数，计算了电子-离子对撞机（EIC）运动学下的不对称性，并讨论其对检验Collins函数普适性和TMD因子化的重要性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 拓展此前对极化pp散射的研究至更理论简洁且互补的极化轻子-质子过程，以更清晰地探测量子色动力学中的横自旋分布（特别是海夸克部分）及Collins函数的普适性。

Method: 采用简化的横动量依赖（TMD）方法，初态取共线构型；使用从半包容深度非弹性散射（SIDIS）和e+e−湮灭中提取的横自旋分布与Collins碎裂函数；在EIC运动学下分别以领头阶（LO）和Weizsäcker-Williams近似下包含准实光子交换进行计算。

Result: 准实光子交换贡献在整个运动学范围内显著但不改变夸克主导通道的主导地位，胶子通道作用微弱；因此Collins不对称性在轻子-质子过程中能更干净地提取横自旋分布，尤其是海夸克成分；该过程为检验Collins函数普适性与TMD因子化提供了新途径。

Conclusion: 极化轻子-质子碰撞中的Collins方位角不对称性是探测横自旋分布（含海夸克）及验证Collins函数普适性与TMD因子化的有力工具，未来EIC实验数据将对此提供关键检验。

Abstract: We study Collins azimuthal asymmetries in pion-in-jet production in polarized lepton-proton collisions, extending previous analyses of polarized $pp$ scattering to a complementary and theoretically simpler process. We keep adopting a simplified transverse momentum dependent (TMD) approach, with a collinear configuration for the initial state, and employ the transversity and Collins fragmentation functions as extracted from semi-inclusive deep inelastic scattering and $e^+ e^-$ annihilation processes. We then compute azimuthal asymmetries for the Electron-Ion Collider (EIC) kinematics, both within a leading order (LO) approach and by including quasireal photon exchange in the Weizsäcker-Williams approximation. Although this contribution is relevant in the whole kinematical range explored, it does not spoil the dominance of quark-initiated channels, leaving only a marginal role to their gluon counterparts. In this respect, Collins asymmetries in lepton-proton processes allow for a much clearer access to the transversity distribution, including its sea-quark component. As we will argue, a comparison with future EIC data could represent a further step in testing the hypothesis of the universality of the Collins function as well as of the TMD factorization for this class of processes.

Since new tetrads whose construction depends on electromagnetic gauge were introduced it has been proved that the physical kinematic nature of spacetime can be altered as proved previously. In this case we will see how to create a field configuration that will reverse the flow of time. <details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用Palatini形式重构爱因斯坦-希尔伯特作用量，引入标量场与里奇标量R的非最小耦合，选取多项式势，利用CosmoLattice进行数值模拟，分析Inflaton场动力学、功率谱、状态方程及原初引力波谱。

Abstract: We investigate the formation of spatially localized, oscillatory in time and non topological solitonic, quasi-stable energy configurations, Oscillons, which are formed at the end of Inflationary epoch, during the preheating phase and decay over long periods of time. Oscillons have been previously studied in literature in the regime of General Relativity using Metric Formalism. In this paper we look for formation of these energy lumps by modifying the gravity part of the Einstein Hilbert Action, considering a non minimal coupling of the scalar field with Ricci Scalar,$R$, and working in an alternative formulation of General Relativity known as Palatini Formalism. The potential we consider is of polynomial form. We demonstrate numerically, using CosmoLattice, that the equation governing the dynamics of the Inflaton scalar field give oscillatory and decaying solutions as it is expected in the case of Oscillons, with power spectrum governing the growth of perturbations of $k$ modes. The equation of state reveals an extended period of Oscillon domination in the early universe. Along with this, the Primordial Gravitational Wave spectrum due to asymmetric distribution of these energy configurations have also been studied. We observe that these generate Ultra-High Frequency regime Gravitational Waves, which lie in the range of the planned future detectors and experiments.

### [97] [Series solutions to the TOV equations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00986)
*Paulo Luz*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Conclusion: 该级数+Padé方法为致密星体建模提供了兼具解析性、灵活性与精度的新范式，不仅深化了对TOV解结构性质的理解，也为多相物态（如夸克-核物质相变）下的星体结构研究提供了可扩展的解析工具。

Abstract: We present general series solutions to the Tolman-Oppenheimer-Volkoff equations for compact stellar objects. We develop an algorithm to compute the coefficients of the power series in terms of the equation of state and its derivatives with respect to the thermodynamic variables. Using these results, we establish general properties of analytic solutions and their relation to the regularity of the equation of state. Applying the theory of Padé approximants, we derive series representations for meromorphic functions whose domains of convergence may include isolated poles. These analytic solutions are then used to obtain closed-form expressions to approximate the radius and mass of stellar objects. We apply the formalism to specific models, namely fluids with affine equations of state and polytropic fluids, and compare the results with those obtained from numerical integration. Lastly, we extend the formalism to piecewise equations of state, deriving series solutions that can be matched across transition hypersurfaces.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 将黑洞建模为测试粒子，解析求解其在薄壳史瓦西可穿越虫洞背景下的径向运动，并计算由质量四极矩及高阶多极矩激发的引力波波形与幅度谱密度。

Result: 获得具有特征性脉冲-间隙结构的引力波信号；该信号在最优取向、距离约500 Mpc内，可落入当前地面引力波探测器（如LIGO/Virgo）的灵敏度范围。

Abstract: We compute the gravitational-wave signal generated by the radial infall of a stellar-mass black hole into a thin-shell Schwarzschild traversable wormhole. Modeling the black hole as a test particle, we derive analytic expressions for the emitted waveform, including contributions from the mass quadrupole and higher-order multipoles. The resulting signal exhibits a characteristic pulse-gap structure associated with repeated throat crossings. We further compute the amplitude spectral density and compare it with representative ground-based detector sensitivities, finding that such signals could lie within the sensitivity range for optimally oriented sources at distances of order ~500 Mpc. These results provide a potential observational signature of traversable wormholes in gravitational-wave data.

### [99] [Photon Spheres and shadow of modified black-hole entropies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01303)
*Fang Liu,Yu-Bo Ma,Yun-Zhi Du,Huai-Fan Li*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文从黑洞热力学第一定律出发，建立了修正熵与度规函数之间的显式对应关系，并利用修正度规计算了光子球半径和阴影大小，发现不同熵修正导致特征性的光学偏移；结合事件视界望远镜对Sgr A*的观测，约束了修正熵中引入的参数范围，为检验广义熵框架及探测对贝肯斯坦-霍金面积律的偏离提供了可行途径。

Method: 从黑洞热力学第一定律出发，建立修正熵与度规函数的对应关系，计算光子球半径和阴影大小，并与EHT对Sgr A*的观测数据对比

Result: 不同熵修正导致特征性光学偏移，并据此约束了修正熵中的参数范围

Conclusion: 该方法为测试广义熵理论和探测量子引力效应提供了可观测的天体物理途径

Abstract: Starting from the first law of black hole thermodynamics, we establish an explicit correspondence between the corrected entropy and the metric function under the condition of fixed black hole energy and horizon position. Using the corrected metric, we further compute the photon sphere radius and shadow size, demonstrating that different entropy corrections lead to characteristic optical shifts. By comparing with the Event Horizon Telescope observations of Sgr A*, we constrain the parameter range introduced in the corrected entropy. This provides a feasible approach for testing generalized entropy frameworks and probing deviations from the Bekenstein-Hawking area law.

Abstract: This manuscript examines viability and stability of anisotropic compact objects in the framework of $f(Q,L_m)$ gravity ($Q$ is the non-metricity and $L_m$ is the matter Lagrangian). We assume a particular functional form of this theory to get explicit expressions for the field equations which govern the behavior of matter and geometry in this context. The configuration of static spherically symmetric structures is evaluated using the two innovative non-singular solutions. We use smooth matching conditions to evaluate the values of unknown constants in the metric coefficients. The viability of considered compact stars is assessed using a graphic analysis of various important physical characteristics. We also investigate stability of the considered stellar objects through sound speed method. It is found that these stellar objects are viable and stable, as all the required conditions are satisfied.

### [101] [Acausal exact vacuum solutions in nonlocal gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01413)
*Zhe Zhao,Leonardo Modesto,Cosimo Bambi*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究非局域引力理论中的经典运动方程，证明一类允许闭合类时曲线的Gödel型宇宙是其真空精确解；该结果仅在特定（尽管广泛）非局域形式因子下成立，表明仅靠可重正化性不足以排除因果律破坏；物质存在可打破Minkowski与Gödel宇宙间的经典简并；非微扰量子层面从平直宇宙跃迁至Gödel宇宙的概率极小。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 检验非局域引力理论是否能避免因果律破坏，特别是探究可重正化性是否足以作为选择合理理论的判据。

Method: 分析非局域引力的经典运动方程，构造并验证Gödel型宇宙作为真空精确解；结合经典与非微扰量子分析，考察因果结构及宇宙学解的稳定性与选择机制。

Result: 发现特定Gödel型宇宙是真空精确解，但仅对一类特殊非局域形式因子成立；物质可打破Minkowski与Gödel宇宙的经典简并；非微扰量子跃迁概率极低。

Conclusion: 可重正化性本身不足以保证因果性；非局域性可能将因果问题从基本尺度放大至宏观尺度；物质和量子效应共同起作用以维持物理合理性。

Abstract: Nonlocal gravity is a promising super-renormalizable or finite quantum gravity theory consistent with unitarity. In this paper, we focus on the classical equations of motion and explicitly show that a particular subclass of Gödel-type Universes, where closed time-like curves are allowed, is an exact solution of nonlocal gravity in vacuum. The result is consistent with a well defined theory at quantum level, but it is realized only with a special, although large, class of nonlocal form factors. Therefore, by itself the renormalizability requirement is not a sufficient guiding principle in vacuum whether we want to avoid the causality violation. From the physical point of view, the causality violation takes place from the non locality fundamental scale to macroscopic scales. Therefore, it is the presence of matter to break the classical degeneracy between the Minkowski and the Gödel Universe. Finally, we have shown that at the non-perturbative quantum level the transition from a flat to a Gödel Universe is ridiculously small.

### [102] [A note on methods for computing the critical curve of Kerr-like black holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01426)
*Siddharth Kumar Sahoo,Indrani Banerjee*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文系统比较了Bardeen、de Vries和Grenzebach等人对Kerr类黑洞临界曲线（‘阴影’）的天球坐标定义，发现三者在真空或远距离观测非均匀等离子体时一致，但在有限距离或均匀等离子体中出现显著分歧；并分析了不同标架（tetrad）对临界曲线的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 澄清不同文献中黑洞阴影（临界曲线）定义之间的差异及其物理适用条件，尤其在等离子体环境和有限距离观测下的不一致性问题。

Method: 系统比较三种临界曲线定义；推导de Vries定义在观测者天球平面上的表达式；分析Grenzebach等人定义与之的差异；研究Bardeen与Carter标架下等离子体中Schwarzschild和Kerr黑洞临界曲线的变化。

Result: 三种定义在远距离、真空/非均匀等离子体下一致；有限距离下Bardeen定义给出最小临界曲线，de Vries给出最大；均匀等离子体中Bardeen定义在远处即偏离另两者且随等离子体密度增加而收缩，与另两者及已有引力透镜结果矛盾；de Vries定义基于观测者天球平面推导；标架改变仅导致临界曲线水平平移。

Conclusion: 黑洞阴影的定义依赖于观测几何与介质环境，Bardeen定义在等离子体中存在物理不合理性；应谨慎选择适用于具体观测场景的定义，并注意标架选择带来的表观偏移。

Abstract: This study systematically compares Bardeen's, de Vries's, and Grenzebach et al.'s celestial coordinate definitions of the critical curve ("shadow") of Kerr-like black holes. We find that all three definitions agree for black holes in vacuum or surrounded by inhomogeneous plasma observed from large distances. However, they diverge for observers located at a finite distance: Bardeen's definition yields the smallest critical curve, while de Vries's yields the largest. When homogeneous plasma is considered, critical curve computed using Bardeen's definition deviates from the other two even at large distances and contracts compared to the vacuum case with increasing plasma density. This is in clear contradiction with the behaviour predicted by de Vries's, Grenzebach et al.'s definitions, and previous gravitational lensing studies. We derive de Vries's definition assuming a critical curve on the observer's sky plane and explain its discrepancy with Grenzebach et al.'s definition. We further explore the effect of the change of tetrad on the critical curve. Using Bardeen and Carter tetrads, we plot the critical curve for Schwarzschild and Kerr black holes in the presence of plasma, highlighting that tetrad changes introduce only a horizontal shift in the critical curve.

Method: 采用贝叶斯定时分析工具Vela处理来自EPTA、NANOGrav及多个射电望远镜的到达时间（ToA）数据，纳入洛伦兹破缺导致的一阶后牛顿保守与耗散修正，并通过后验重采样将参数约束映射至理论基本耦合常数。

Abstract: We constrain Einstein-aether gravity -- a Lorentz-violating extension of General Relativity in which a dynamical, unit timelike vector field selects a preferred frame -- using updated high-precision pulsar timing observations of PSR J1738+0333 from EPTA second Data Release and the NANOGrav 9-year release, in combination with ToAs from Arecibo, Green Bank, Nancay, Parkes, and Westerbork. Our method accounts for both conservative and dissipative first post-Newtonian corrections arising from Lorentz violation; here we apply it to PSR J1738+0333 using the Bayesian timing pipeline Vela to process the full ToA dataset. We sample the joint posterior over binary component masses, post-Keplerian parameters and center-of-mass velocity components, and then apply a resampling scheme to propagate posteriors into robust constraints on the fundamental theory parameters, obtaining the most stringent strong-field bounds on the Einstein-aether coupling constants from a single binary pulsar system to date.

Method: 基于洛伦兹几何与变分法，对类光曲线空间的拓扑与微分结构进行分析，给出费马原理在光滑类光曲线下的严格证明，并探讨二次到达时间泛函等替代变分框架及其在多重性结果中的应用。

Abstract: This paper presents a survey of the Fermat principle within the framework of general relativity, tracing its evolution from classical optics to its modern variational formulation in Lorentzian geometry. In particular, we provide its proof in the framework of smooth lightlike curves. We also analyze the mathematical difficulties inherent in the relativistic setting, specifically demonstrating that the space of lightlike curves in the Sobolev topology does not admit a smooth manifold structure due to the cone nature of the null condition. To address these variational obstacles, we discuss alternative frameworks highlighting the role of the quadratic arrival time functional in establishing multiplicity results for light rays. Furthermore, we explore significant extensions of the principle, such as its application to extended sources and receivers, arbitrary arrival curves, timelike geodesics with prescribed proper time, Finsler spacetimes, or settings with a non-continuous interface giving rise to a Snell law.

### [105] [Relational quantum dynamics of the black hole interior: singularity resolution and quantum bounce](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01576)
*Paolo Fragolino,Saeed Rastgoo*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文通过完全关系性和规范不变的量子化框架研究了Schwarzschild黑洞内部（等距于Kantowski-Sachs宇宙模型），利用改进代数量子化构建物理希尔伯特空间，并借助Page-Wootters形式和协变POVM时钟实现量子动力学；构造并计算了面积、Kretschmann标量和零测地线膨胀标量等规范不变关系观测量，发现奇点被消除，出现黑洞到白洞的量子反弹。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决广义相对论中黑洞内部奇点问题，探索量子引力下黑洞内部结构及奇点是否可被量子效应消解。

Method: 采用完全关系性与规范不变的量子化框架，用精炼代数量子化构建物理希尔伯特空间，结合Page-Wootters形式与基于构型变量的协变POVM时钟描述量子演化；通过群平均（G-twirl）构造规范不变关系观测量。

Result: Kretschmann标量和膨胀标量在整个黑洞内保持有限；2-球面面积存在非零下界（正比于系统变量的不确定性）；膨胀标量在量子反弹点处变号，标志黑洞向白洞转变；奇点消解源于关系性、海森堡不确定性原理及物理希尔伯特空间结构。

Conclusion: 黑洞内部奇点可在不依赖特定量子化方案的前提下，由关系性、量子不确定性与物理态空间结构自然消解，支持黑洞-白洞量子跃迁图像。

Abstract: We study the interior of the Schwarzschild black hole which is isometric to the Kantowski-Sachs cosmological model, using a fully relational and gauge-invariant quantization framework. The physical Hilbert space is constructed via refined algebraic quantization, and quantum dynamics is recovered through the Page-Wootters formalism with a covariant POVM clock built from one of the two configuration variables, whose Hamiltonian is proportional to the momentum of the said variable. Gauge-invariant relational observables for the area of 2-spheres, the Kretschmann scalar, and the expansion scalar of null geodesic are constructed via group averaging (G-twirl) and evaluated on physical states. We find that the Kretschmann and expansion scalars remain finite throughout the black hole, while the area of 2-spheres is bounded below by a minimum value proportional to the uncertainty in the system variable, which is the other configuration variable distinct from the clock variable. In particular, the expansion scalar vanishes and changes sign at the quantum bounce, establishing a black-hole-to-white-hole transition. These results hold for any general clock whose operator forms a canonical pair with the clock Hamiltonian, and require no specific quantization scheme other than the Schrodinger representation. The singularity resolution emerges directly from relationality, the Heisenberg uncertainty principle, and the structure of the physical Hilbert space.

Abstract: We investigate traversable wormhole solutions within a four-dimensional effective theory derived from a five-dimensional Einstein-Maxwell-Chern-Simons action with a non-minimally coupled scalar field. A warped Kaluza-Klein compactification yields an Einstein-frame theory containing a phantom dilaton, a canonical axion, a Maxwell field, and a Kaluza-Klein vector, with the couplings fixed by the higher-dimensional origin. Focusing on the Ellis-Bronnikov geometry, we construct solutions that incorporate both dyonic Maxwell and Kaluza-Klein fields. We obtain a systematic classification of configurations, ranging from the pure phantom-supported wormhole to fully coupled dilaton-axion-gauge configurations. The Kaluza-Klein sector enriches the solution space with additional structure while preserving analytic tractability. These results show that regular, asymptotically flat traversable four-dimensional wormholes arise naturally from higher-dimensional scalar-tensor theories.

### [107] [Reevaluation of Inflationary Dynamics in Extended General Relativity with Perturbatively and Tensorially Structured Conformal Metric](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01619)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决标准暴胀理论中暴胀子身份不明、势能起源不清以及量子引力作用不明确等根本性问题。

Method: 采用一种既具微扰结构又具张量结构的量子变形共形度规，重新分析暴胀动力学，并推导包含谱指数、跑动、张标比等在内的完整可观测量解析表达式。

Result: 建立了封闭且自洽的标量与张量功率谱及其谱倾角、跑动和张标比等的解析公式；量子修正具有明确物理含义（测度缩放与动量诱导动能变形），并以可控、可预测方式修改暴胀可观测量。
